The \"Cards\" is on the left-hand side of the app to reference a list of customers, inventory items and pricing. You can reference the \"Cards\" to add inventory items onto the \"Paper\" (which is the invoice) on the right. We gleaned this metaphor from previous experiences where we successfully helped fast-growing companies transform their on the go manual \"Cards-and-Paper\" invoice issuance to that of a fully automated one using our software.
